getDataSourceFromQuery(ctx context.Context, user identity.Requester, skipDSCache bool, query *simplejson.Json, history map[string]*datasources.DataSource) (*datasources.DataSource, error) {\n   430→\tvar err error\n   431→\tuid := query.Get(\"datasource\").Get(\"uid\").MustString()\n   432→\n   433→\t// before 8.3 special types could be sent as datasource (expr)\n   434→\tif uid == \"\" {\n 443→\n   444→\tif kind := expr.NodeTypeFromDatasourceUID(uid); kind != expr.TypeDatasourceNode {\n   445→\t\treturn expr.DataSourceModelFromNodeType(kind)\n   446→\t}\n   447→\n   448→\tif uid == https://github.com/golang/go/blob/dc04f3ba1f25313bc9c97e728620206c235db9ee/src/net/http/httputil/reverseproxy.go#L411-L421\n   302→func removeConnectionHeaders(h map[string][]string) {\n   303→\tfor 312→\t\t\t}\n   313→\t\t}\n   314→\t}\n   315→}\n   316→\n   317→// Hop-by-hop headers. These are removed when sent to the backend.\n   318→// As of RFC 7230, hop-by-hop headers are required to appear in the\n   319→// Connection header field. These are the headers defined by the\n   320→// obsoleted RFC 2616 (section 13.5.1) and are used for backward\n   321→// compatibility.\n   322→//\n   323→// Copied from https://github.com/golang/go/blob/dc04f3ba1f25313bc9c97e728620206c235db9ee/src/net/http/httputil/reverseproxy.go#L171-L186\n   324→var hopHeaders = []string{\n   325→\t\"Connection\",\n   326→\t\"Proxy-Connection\", // non-standard but still sent by libcurl and rejected by e.g. google\n   327→\t\"Keep-Alive\",\n   328→\t\"Proxy-Authenticate\",\n   329→\t\"Proxy-Authorization\",\n   330→\t\"Te\",      // canonicalized version of \"TE\"\n   331→\t\"Trailer\", // not Trailers per URL above; https://www.rfc-editor.org/errata_search.php?eid=4522\n   332→\t\"Transfer-Encoding\",\n   333→\t\"Upgrade\",\n   334→\t\"User-Agent\",\n   335→}\n   336→\n   337→// removeHopByHopHeaders removes hop-by-hop headers. Especially\n   338→// important is \"Connection\" because we want a persistent\n   339→// connection, regardless of what the client sent to us.\n   340→//\n   341→// Based on https://github.com/golang/go/blob/dc04f3ba1f25313bc9c97e728620206c235db9ee/src/net/http/httputil/reverseproxy.go#L276-L281\n   342→func removeHopByHopHeaders(h map[string][]string) {\n   343→\tfor _, hh := range hopHeaders {\n   344→\t\tfor k := range h {\n   345→\t\t\tif hh == textproto.CanonicalMIMEHeaderKey(k) {\n   346→\t\t\t\tdelete(h, k)\n   347→\t\t\t\tbreak\n   348→\t\t\t}\n   349→\t\t}\n   350→\t}\n   351→}\n   352→\n   353→func removeNonAllowedHeaders(h map[string][]string) {\n   354→\tfor k := range h {\n   355→\t\tif textproto.CanonicalMIMEHeaderKey(k) == setCookieHeaderName {\n   356→\t\t\tdelete(h, k)\n   357→\t\t}\n   358→\t}\n   359→}\n   360→\n   361→// ensureContentTypeHeader makes sure a content type always is returned in response.\n   362→func ensureContentTypeHeader(res *backend.CallResourceResponse) {\n   363→\tif res == nil {\n   364→\t\treturn\n   365→\t}\n   366→\n   367→\tvar hasContentType bool\n   368→\tfor k := range res.Headers {\n   369→\t\tif textproto.CanonicalMIMEHeaderKey(k) == contentTypeHeaderName {\n   370→\t\t\thasContentType = true\n   371→\t\t\tbreak\n   372→\t\t}\n   373→\t}\n   374→\n   375→\tif !hasContentType && res.Status != http.StatusNoContent {\n   376→\t\tres.Headers[contentTypeHeaderName] = []string{defaultContentType}\n   377→\t}\n   378→}\n   379→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware.
